) AS [t0] ON [p].[Id] = [t0].[ProductId]

    SELECT [p2].[Id], [p2].[CreatedDate], [p2].[ProductId], [p2].[TagId], [t2].[Id] AS [Id0], [t2].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [t2].[Name]
    FROM [ProductTags] AS [p2]
    INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [t2] ON [p2].[TagId] = [t2].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [c].[Id], [b].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [t1].[Id]

FROM [Products] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [p].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p0] ON [p].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[Id], [p1].[ColorId], [p1].[CreatedDate], [p1].[ProductId], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [c0].[Name]
    FROM [ProductColors] AS [p1]
    INNER JOIN [Colors] AS [c0] ON [p1].[ColorId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p2].[Id], [p2].[CreatedDate], [p2].[ProductId], [p2].[TagId], [t1].[Id] AS [Id0], [t1].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [t1].[Name]
    FROM [ProductTags] AS [p2]
    INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [t1] ON [p2].[TagId] = [t1].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [p].[Id] = [t0].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [c].[Id], [b].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t0].[Id]

FROM (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedDate], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Stock]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [t].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [t].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p0] ON [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[Id], [p1].[ColorId], [p1].[CreatedDate], [p1].[ProductId], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [c0].[Name]
    FROM [ProductColors] AS [p1]
    INNER JOIN [Colors] AS [c0] ON [p1].[ColorId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p2].[Id], [p2].[CreatedDate], [p2].[ProductId], [p2].[TagId], [t2].[Id] AS [Id0], [t2].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [t2].[Name]
    FROM [ProductTags] AS [p2]
    INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [t2] ON [p2].[TagId] = [t2].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[ProductId]

SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedDate], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Stock], [c].[Id], [c].[CreatedDate], [c].[Image], [c].[Name], [b].[Id], [b].[CreatedDate], [b].[Image], [b].[Name], [p0].[Id], [p0].[CreatedDate], [p0].[Img], [p0].[IsMain], [p0].[ProductId], [t].[Id], [t].[ColorId], [t].[CreatedDate], [t].[ProductId], [t].[Id0], [t].[CreatedDate0], [t].[Name], [t0].[Id], [t0].[CreatedDate], [t0].[ProductId], [t0].[TagId], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[CreatedDate0], [t0].[Name]
FROM [Products] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [p].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p0] ON [p].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[Id], [p1].[ColorId], [p1].[CreatedDate], [p1].[ProductId], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [c0].[Name]
    FROM [ProductColors] AS [p1]
    INNER JOIN [Colors] AS [c0] ON [p1].[ColorId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p2].[Id], [p2].[CreatedDate], [p2].[ProductId], [p2].[TagId], [t1].[Id] AS [Id0], [t1].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [t1].[Name]
    FROM [ProductTags] AS [p2]
    INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [t1] ON [p2].[TagId] = [t1].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [p].[Id] = [t0].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [c].[Id], [b].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t0].[Id]
